<div id="review_38920855" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/38920855" />
    <a title="Holly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1671402-holly"><img alt="Holly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296879358p2/1671402.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/38920855?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Holly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Holly" href="/user/show/1671402-holly">Holly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1671402-holly?shelf=kresley-cole">kresley-cole</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer38920855" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13316876800566344536">I'll start by saying that while I really liked Rydstrom, Sabine made this book for me. I loved her. She was hilarious and witty and I loved her attitude. Her zingers were some of the best that Kresley Cole has delivered to date. She was definitely a bad sorceress but she wasn't an evil one. She was just looking out for numero uno and woe to anyone else standing in her way. I loved her sister too, and am breathlessly waiting for the moment when she has her own story. <br/><br/>Rydstrom was so deliciously s</span>
  <span id="freeText13316876800566344536" style="display:none">I'll start by saying that while I really liked Rydstrom, Sabine made this book for me. I loved her. She was hilarious and witty and I loved her attitude. Her zingers were some of the best that Kresley Cole has delivered to date. She was definitely a bad sorceress but she wasn't an evil one. She was just looking out for numero uno and woe to anyone else standing in her way. I loved her sister too, and am breathlessly waiting for the moment when she has her own story. <br /><br />Rydstrom was so deliciously stuffy in this book and he had a serious stick up his butt. When he does loosen up though it wasn't in an, "Oh yay, he's finally loosening up" sort of way. It was, "Oh My God, he's lost his mind!" The problem with being a rage demon, is well, the rage. Sabine has him imprisoned in his own dungeon and her methods of ensuring his compliance are akin to waving a red flag in a bulls face, or better yet, kicking a bull in the nuts and then trying to run away to safety before said bull recovers in time to run you down. Let's just say payback's a bitch. I also loved reading the same scenes from Dark Desires After Dusk (Cade &amp; Holly's story) but from Rydstrom and Sabine's perspective. Especially that scene when Cade comes by his house to drop off the sword. It was really funny. <br /><br />My only problem with this book is that it was too long. It needed to be trimmed. Rydstrom and Sabine's constant back and forth was exhausting. All their teasing and lack of follow through was getting to me and it seemed to drag on, but then when things got really good towards the end it seemed to fly by at a lightening fast pace. But here's a really fun fact, Nix is taking a time-out in order to inspect the Lords of The Underworld! I wonder who she will be joined up with? And if that will mesh well? She is like Anya so it shouldn't be too jarring to get someone like Nix transplanted into Gena Showalter's world. It will be interesting at any rate. <br /><br />Anyhoo, love this book, wish it was a little shorter and now I have an enormous girl crush on Sabine. This was yet another great addition to the Immortals After Dark series and I'm already greedily looking forward to the next one. Enjoy! 4.5 stars. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13316876800566344536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25694252-kiss-of-a-demon-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70492479-mara?shelf=ebook-owned">ebook-owned</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2275721284" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10115739853809461386">3.5 stars -- This is a book that had a lot of guts to it, which I admire, and there were parts of it that I enjoyed. Most notably Sabine... she's a really complicated protagonist, and in Romancelandia, it's rare that an author is willing to "go there" in portraying what a person who has had to scrap for everything in life whilst undergoing extreme domestic abuse (and literally dying multiple times ffs). She's NOT going to be all smiles & roses coming out of that, and I really enjoyed spending ti</span>
  <span id="freeText10115739853809461386" style="display:none">3.5 stars -- This is a book that had a lot of guts to it, which I admire, and there were parts of it that I enjoyed. Most notably Sabine... she's a really complicated protagonist, and in Romancelandia, it's rare that an author is willing to "go there" in portraying what a person who has had to scrap for everything in life whilst undergoing extreme domestic abuse (and literally dying multiple times ffs). She's NOT going to be all smiles &amp; roses coming out of that, and I really enjoyed spending time with her as a lead. She had a lot of emotional depth, and I thought she was one of the most interesting heroines I've read in a long time.<br />That said, this is a true hate to love situation and that part of the book was just hard for me to get into. I think the ending sold me on the relationship as a whole, but there was a lot of underlying consent issues that were hard for me to get my head around. I think if it was more explicitly positioned as a dubcon kind of book, maybe it would have made more sense to me? On top of that, I think there are some plot "conveniences," let's say, that she didn't totally sell me on. <br />Still, for the heroine alone, I will say this was an above average PNR, so I think 3.5 stars feels right</span>

    <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth"><img alt="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487525094p2/13870608.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/470653358?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=gods-come-out-to-play">gods-come-out-to-play</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer470653358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14351288284094726537"><b>4 Illusionary stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403391097i/10087900._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Illusion is Reality's coy lover who cheers him when he is grim. Illusion is cunning to his wisdom of ages, weet oblivion to his knowledge. A bounty to his lack.</i>
</b> <br/><br/>This book's best feature is Sabine by far. I love that Kresley Cole creates characters that, though they're not all bad at heart(mostly), still have some wickedness and are unapologetic about it. Sabine is one of these characters, she is shelfish, arrogant and ruthless. I absolutely love her.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"She may be an evil</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText14351288284094726537" style="display:none"><b>4 Illusionary stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403391097i/10087900._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Illusion is Reality's coy lover who cheers him when he is grim. Illusion is cunning to his wisdom of ages, weet oblivion to his knowledge. A bounty to his lack.</i>
</b> <br><br>This book's best feature is Sabine by far. I love that Kresley Cole creates characters that, though they're not all bad at heart(mostly), still have some wickedness and are unapologetic about it. Sabine is one of these characters, she is shelfish, arrogant and ruthless. I absolutely love her.<br><br><b>
  <i>"She may be an evil bitch, but she is my evil bitch and I'll have no other..."</i>
</b><br><br>Rydstrom is the perceived do-gooder, the benevolent ruler, the kind leader, the inspirational king. To be honest I am not completely sold on him. I think all his honesty and honor is just on paper, I never actually saw it on action, at least not at the degree the book tries to sell it to us.<br><br>My general idea of this book was "too-much-built up", "too-little-deliverance". There are all these actions leading here, so much pain from Cadeon, so many difficulties for Rydstrom, so hard a life for Sabine and so much steam rising between Ry and Sab and in the end there is no "boom". It's all solved way too easily and quickly.<br><br>Still the book is great, Sabine awesome and Ry hot!<br><br><b>
  <i>“Sabine gave a Scoff. "I could be virtuous, if I wanted to be."<br>In an incredulous tone, he said, "You don't know the meaning of virtue!"<br>"Of course I do - it means your thong must be white.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>Re-read it as part of the IAD series Read-A-Long with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/100383-league-of-lusty-ladies" rel="nofollow noopener">League of Lusty Ladies</a>.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14351288284094726537" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer69537584" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10708718468624649027">I really ended up liking this in the end, as well as Sabine who I hated when I started this book. Happily, everything turned great after the middle, but still, I felt like those first 200 pages were a bit too much and to slow. Who wants 200 pages of foreplay after all? <br/><br/>I didn't like this book as much as Cade's -which I upgraded to 5 stars after reading this- and to be honest, I expected more from Rydstrom. He was the one who stood out since Bowen's book, the serious, brooding, tormented but stoi</span>
  <span id="freeText10708718468624649027" style="display:none">I really ended up liking this in the end, as well as Sabine who I hated when I started this book. Happily, everything turned great after the middle, but still, I felt like those first 200 pages were a bit too much and to slow. Who wants 200 pages of foreplay after all? <br /><br />I didn't like this book as much as Cade's -which I upgraded to 5 stars after reading this- and to be honest, I expected more from Rydstrom. He was the one who stood out since Bowen's book, the serious, brooding, tormented but stoic and calm king. In his book though, it was Sabine who stole the show, for better or worse, while he was left backstage. I enjoyed reading this -at least the second part- but where characters are concerned, I think Rydstrom was underdeveloped. Sabine was another matter; I started off hating her and then couldn't help laughing at her lines. <br /><br />I just wish Cole will write Melanthe's story with Thronos; I'd buy that one in a second!</span>

<div id="review_1736788372" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1736788372" />
    <a title="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5252054-irena"><img alt="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425497470p2/5252054.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1736788372?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" href="/user/show/5252054-irena">ᴥ Irena ᴥ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=wizards-mages-or-sorcerers">wizards-mages-or-sorcerers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=parallel-universe-other-dimension">parallel-universe-other-dimension</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1736788372" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4806217858877955650">Finally, a female protagonist I liked! After the previous book and its annoying (I'm being nice here) heroine, I went into this story with low expectations. <br/>What I wanted is to see Rydstrom Woede fall and go crazy a bit. He was not my favourite person in the previous book because I quite liked his brother. I felt sorry for Cadeon. I was not disappointed. You get that and more and I loved him for it.<br/><br/>I already know how Sabine trapped Rydstrom and here you see what happened in that dungeon in Torni</span>
  <span id="freeText4806217858877955650" style="display:none">Finally, a female protagonist I liked! After the previous book and its annoying (I'm being nice here) heroine, I went into this story with low expectations. <br />What I wanted is to see Rydstrom Woede fall and go crazy a bit. He was not my favourite person in the previous book because I quite liked his brother. I felt sorry for Cadeon. I was not disappointed. You get that and more and I loved him for it.<br /><br />I already know how Sabine trapped Rydstrom and here you see what happened in that dungeon in Tornin. She kept him just long enough for me to start thinking I'd like a change of scenery now, thanks. It's not a spoiler since it's in the blurb and if you've read the previous book, you know they end up in his house in New Orleans at one point. However, the journey there is pretty entertaining. What happens after that is even better.<br /> Both Sabine and Rydstrom have a turn of being <i>in charge</i>. I can't remember the last time I've read about a paranormal couple matched this well. <br /><br />What surprised me the most is how much I loved Sabine. She is truly a great character. She doesn't change a lot in the course of the story. Even when she is vulnerable, she is strong. I seem to be in the minority of readers who like their female characters <i>feminine</i> (blasphemy today as far as I can see). <br />Sabine's relationship with Lanthe, her sister, is one of the highlights of the story and her character. <br />It is so rare I read a paranormal story and actually see why someone would love that particular female protagonist. She even proves it with her unexpected reaction to something Rydstrom did earlier.<br /><br />I skimmed over most of the sex scenes or rather read them but haven’t paid too much attention. They weren't that interesting, but the rest of it was good.<br /><br />With most of these books you get a beginning of another story, maybe even two. <br />Lanthe and Sabine spent hundreds of years running away from angel-like beings and Lanthe's story will be about them. I expect a lot of heartbreak there.<br />Next, one of the books in the series is called 'Lothaire'. I think this is the first time the vampire makes an appearance in this world.<br /><br />Overall, <i>Kiss of a Demon King</i> is not perfect, but Sabine deserves a star of her own so there's that.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4806217858877955650" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3204412473212311587"><b>Reread Review August 10, 2017 </b><br/><br/>4 1/2 "Battle Royal" Stars!<br/><br/>Another very fun reread. Theses two had a serious battle of wills going on. The sexual mind games were epic. Really it got a little bit old after a while. But then finally the stubbornness on both parts broke just enough and the book got really good. The first 50-ish% was ok. The last 50-ish% was really good.   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/98251189?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="DarienMoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="DarienMoya" href="/user/show/3069494-darienmoya">DarienMoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3069494-darienmoya?shelf=2010-reads">2010-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3069494-darienmoya?shelf=demon">demon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer98251189" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6519083922360515310"> ^^GOTTA LOVE DEMON KISSES!^^<br/><br/>My least favourite book, but still another solid instalment in this wonderful, erotic and edgy series. I was hoping for like the read of all reads for Rydstrom book, but I wasn’t overly impressed maybe I just expected too much for him because of the build-up and all the things involving him throughout the series.<br/><br/><b>THE RUNDOWN</b>- Rydstrom is a king who lost his kingdom and is fighting hell and high-water to get it back. Problem, the person living in his castle and terrori</span>
  <span id="freeText6519083922360515310" style="display:none"> ^^GOTTA LOVE DEMON KISSES!^^<br /><br />My least favourite book, but still another solid instalment in this wonderful, erotic and edgy series. I was hoping for like the read of all reads for Rydstrom book, but I wasn’t overly impressed maybe I just expected too much for him because of the build-up and all the things involving him throughout the series.<br /><br /><b>THE RUNDOWN</b>- Rydstrom is a king who lost his kingdom and is fighting hell and high-water to get it back. Problem, the person living in his castle and terrorizing his people is all but invincible, so that is proving problematic. Some very interesting news came around saying there is a sword that just might slay his nemesis; and he will be able to rule over his people once more. Ryd needs it bad, like a plant needs water in hottest dessert. On his way to obtain the sword, he is intercepted, captured and held prisoner by a crazed but very attractive woman. He is being held in the dungeons of his own bloody castle, talk about the effin nerve of this woman. Seems this is the Queen of Illusions and she just might be his woman. Go figure!<br /><br /><b>SABINE</b>- Two words “crazy bitch” but you gotta love her. She knows that Rydstrom is her fated man, because it has been prophesized. All she has to do is get his vow that she will be queen and make a baby. Easier said than done, she desperately needs this so she can finally be free of her evil and creepy brother. Also, she very much wishes to stop dying and live peacefully with her sister. Laying with a demon is a sacrifice she just has to make, because everyone knows demons are the lowest. Well Sabine is about to be educated in sexy, horns, and the hottest male she has ever seen. This might not be so bad after all, if only he didn’t hate her so much.<br /><br /><b>RYDSTROM</b>- This guy carries the world on his shoulders; if you saw him, you would see the world. He blames himself for everything; he is a little bit uptight, and very serious. When the opportunity to finally claim his birthright arises, he wants it bad. So the woman who is holding him captive he wants nothing more than to rip her pretty little head off. If the prophecy that she is claiming, is true by chance. Then this woman is his mate, his queen and he hates her guts. Yet his body wants her real bad, but he must not lose sight of what is important, his people and kingdom.<br /><br /><b>PLOT</b>- I think it was the reawakening of two people, both facing very different obstacles. Through the foreplay, and adventure they both come to realize what it is they really want. Ryd has to get that sword and he has to fight for his woman, Sabine has to trust this demon and hope. It clearly was a look into this larger than life demon that so intrigued us, and his falling in love. Another is the budding relationship between Sabine and Ryd, let me tell you it is no easy road. I am pretty sure they wanted to murder each other at times, and things was just all the more difficult because they could never see eye to eye. Sabine can be exasperating.<br /><br /><b>FEELINGS</b>- Not my fave but I still loved it, Sabine clearly is a little nuts but she was entertaining. I enjoyed Ryd and it was nice to see things from his point of view, I always thought he was a little bit of a bastard and needed to move and forgive his brother Cadeon. This book was very sexy, all the things these two got up to was epic. At some point, I was severely frustrated, I was like let each other cum already, and stop wasting time. I loved Sabine with the little demon boy I think those were some of her best moments, warmed my heart. I thought the ending was a little abrupt but I do appreciate there was no 100% turn over for both characters, Ryd is still uptight and Sabine is still just as selfish and nutty but she is getting there.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6519083922360515310" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61221433-theresa?shelf=kresley-cole-books">kresley-cole-books</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1900498288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer535267145273295170">A tug of war love story between the righteous Demon King Rydstrom and the morally compromised (Perhaps Misunderstood??) Sorceress Sabine... a seductive battle of wills to see who will yield first to the overwhelming passion that drives their questionable methods... both battling for their prizes, neither truly knowing the worth of the bounty, these two go to the extreme edge of desire and want to fulfill their quest... both of these characters exert their stubbornness, strong mindsets, free will</span>
  <span id="freeText535267145273295170" style="display:none">A tug of war love story between the righteous Demon King Rydstrom and the morally compromised (Perhaps Misunderstood??) Sorceress Sabine... a seductive battle of wills to see who will yield first to the overwhelming passion that drives their questionable methods... both battling for their prizes, neither truly knowing the worth of the bounty, these two go to the extreme edge of desire and want to fulfill their quest... both of these characters exert their stubbornness, strong mindsets, free will, and powerful belief systems that clash with one another leading to a true opposites attract dilemma; add in an intense chemistry and you have the making of an explosive storyline... I both enjoyed and loathed these characters; each acted in despicable ways, yet at times both appeared vulnerable, humorous, and endearing; the mix of characteristics actually softened me to both characters and their powerful personalities... I appreciated the tie in to the previous novel in the series (Cadeon's story) flowing effortlessly between storylines and allowing the reader to bridge the gaps in the flow of the story... a deliciously sinful story from start to finish (and as always, I loved the character of Nix!)... 4.5 Stars!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1350556411337521602">Intended for a mature audience.<br/>Sorry, but these stories are too predictable. Star-crossed lovers will find each other at long last. The male will have waited an eternity for this. The female will resist the relationship, or keep secrets from intended male. And, the guy will always be well endowed, and wealthy beyond belief. They will consummate their love toward the end of the book with the exchange of vows, and will only say the L word after a near death experience has occurred. <br/>So far, this is</span>
  <span id="freeText1350556411337521602" style="display:none">Intended for a mature audience.<br />Sorry, but these stories are too predictable. Star-crossed lovers will find each other at long last. The male will have waited an eternity for this. The female will resist the relationship, or keep secrets from intended male. And, the guy will always be well endowed, and wealthy beyond belief. They will consummate their love toward the end of the book with the exchange of vows, and will only say the L word after a near death experience has occurred. <br />So far, this is the trend. I really enjoyed the first four books in the series... but now, even the romantic scenes fall flat. Please, stop using the word buck in bed. It's not sexy. It reminds me of a bucking bronco. <br />I still haven't given up on this series yet. It's like eating junk food. I tell myself, ok, enough of this, but then I wonder what the next book is like, and I read it. <br /> <br /><br /> </span>

Well this book is what happens when those still waters are installed into a sexy demon king and then a hand grenade aka Sabine Queen of Illsions is thrown in them!   <span id="freeText4764409179994439000" style="display:none">You know that saying that still waters run deep? Well this book is what happens when those still waters are installed into a sexy demon king and then a hand grenade aka Sabine Queen of Illsions is thrown in them! Needless to say the results are explosive!<br /><br />Rydstrom is hands down the sexiest demon EVER, and I loved his book, I know this is quite a few peoples least favourite, but they must all be crazy. The sexual tension, the sexy Rydstrom, the action, the hot as hell Rydstrom, a smart ass heroine who has become my favourite female in the series and oh did I mention the extremely lickable Rydstrom?<br /><br />As I mentioned above, Sabine has become my favourite female in the series, she was funny and slightly evil, although I think survivor is probably a more apt description of her. <br /><br />This book was really great and another great addition to the Immortals after Dark series which seems to be getting better and better.<br /><br />I am trying to think of my favourite quote, but there are just so damn many! So here are a few:<br /><br /><i>"Blah, blah, blah. Demon boy, I can't speak that language. Furthermore, I don't want to pollute my brain by learning it. So it's time for you to learn mine. First lesson-I'm Say-been. I'm oft described as byoo-tee-full and mah-jest'ick."<br /><br />"You know, do nice shite for her. Buy her things. Really think about what she likes and what makes her happy and make it happen. She'll come around. And if she doesn't, you can cut off your horns for her. Chicks dig that." <br /><br />In an incredulous tone, he said, "You don't know the meaning of virtue!"<br />"Of course I do-it means your thong must be white."</i></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vx1e6Dg07ZdChIXfyHYHUdIy768lhdwjLH4LzxrLpreM5ArmVr3aqBj0wj3e/FDCeUv6Qgpq9DjCyJXAixeLhg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12898267000888597222">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br/><br/>A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br/>Her IAD bo</span>
  <span id="freeText12898267000888597222" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family. Learn more about Kresley at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kresleycole.com">www.kresleycole.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thearcanachronicles.com">www.thearcanachronicles.com</a><br /><br /></span>
